把时间当作朋友（第3版）

李笑来

528个笔记

内容简介

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

当你把时间花在一个人身上的时候，相当于在他的身上倾注了你生命的一段，不管最终结果如何，反正，那个人、那件事都成了你生命的一部分——不管最后你是喜欢还是不喜欢。

阅读说明

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

很多“时间管理技巧”并非无用，但往往由于使用者心智能力低下甚至尚未开启心智，致使那些技巧只能治标，不能治本，甚至既不治标，也不治本。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

成功从来都不是人人都可以做到的事情，过去不是，现在不是，将来依然不是。基于比较的成功观，是伤人的、害人的。事实上，对年轻人来说，成长比成功更重要，而且，这才是人人都可以做到的事情，才是人人都值得追求的事情。而成长其实只有一条路——积累。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这本书里没有安慰，因为这本书不是写给脆弱的人的——只有脆弱的人才不断需要安慰。现实是残酷的，生活是艰难的，无论什么样的时代，无论对哪一个层次的人，都是如此，对大多数年轻人来说，更是如此。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人的理性建立在接受现实的基础上，不能接受现实，一切成长都是虚妄。

再版前言

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

用正确的方法做正确的事情

第1版前言

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要管理的不是时间，而是自己。

2．慌乱

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

既勤奋又懒惰

3．解决

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人们很难接受与已有知识和经验相左的信息或观念，因为一个人已有的知识和观念都是经过反复筛选的。尽管很多知识和观念是被灌输的，但知识的持有者对“被灌输”这一事实往往毫无察觉，就算察觉，也可能拒绝承认。人们更愿意相信自己拥有一定的判断能力，不会被轻易糊弄。即使是一些“想当然”的观念，人们也倾向于认为那是“思考过后的结论”。

1．孰主孰仆

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

不再让自己“跟着感觉走”，成为大脑的奴隶，而是翻身做大脑的主人。

2．何谓心智

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一个人的心智就是其过往获得的一切知识及经验的总和（包括基于这些知识和经验造就的思考方法、思考模式）。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

心智与智商不同。大多数人都拥有正常的智商，但并非每个拥有正常智商的人都拥有正常的心智。许多人的心智仍处于未开启的状态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一个道理明明非常正确，却因为讲述道理的人由于某件事情被戳穿，露出伪君子的嘴脸，而使很多人不再相信那个原本应该被笃信的道理。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“做事只要踏实、认真，事业就会做大”，这原本是非常朴素而又正确的道理，可偏偏整天把这句话挂在嘴边[插图]的唐骏[插图]被人揭出老底——他的学历是假的，他可一点都不踏实！于是，很多人“开窍”了，“顿悟”了，得出结论：“再也不相信这种鬼话了！”

1．速成绝无可能

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

期望速成，从微观层面上看，有两个主要原因。第一个原因是人希望自己的欲望马上得到满足的天性。一

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

从这个角度更进一步地说，大多数人都抱着类似这样的想法：如果收获的可能性很大，最好马上看到成果；如果收获的可能性很小，最好马上知道结果。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

第二个原因，也是浮躁的根源，就是很多人不懂“有些阶段就是无法跨越”这个道理。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

总的来说，一方面是自己的欲望无限，一方面是要完成的事情太多，一方面是自我满意度的不断下降——这就是人们总是不由自主地期望速成的根源。出路肯定存在，但这出路只有一个起点——接受现实。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我有不足，我需要时间，我没办法一蹴而就。

2．交换才是硬道理

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

大多数人之所以会浮躁，是因为他们一无积累（或者积累太少，几乎无法换取任何东西），二无方法和经验（所以求而不得）。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

拿出一张纸，将其划分为左右两半，然后做两个列表，左边是“我有的”，右边是“我要的”，逐一罗列。完成后要尽量客观地判断：先划掉“我要的”当中那些无法用“我有的”换取的；再仔细判断在剩下的能用“我有的”换取的那些“我要的”之中，哪些是必须的、必要的、重要的、不可或缺的，并在其上做重点标记。偶尔会有一些“我要的”无法用现在“我有的”换得，却又是必须、必要，甚至不可或缺的，这需要我们认真考虑用什么样的手段再积累一些“我有的”，从而有足够的资本换取那些“暂时换不到但极其想要的”——或努力勤奋，或投机取巧。投机的方式并非不能用，尽管它的成功概率实际上并没有看起来那么高，而它的失败概率甚至和它看起来的成功概率一样高。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

还有一个辅助手段，就是在想到“我要什么”的时候马上提醒自己，接下来要花一些时间去思考“我有什么”。

3．完美永不存在

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

做咨询工作的人都有深刻的体验：客户的常识越少，要求越高——因为不懂，所以会随便提要求。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

把自己标榜成完美主义者，是他们抬高自己的手段，是他们不去做一些事情的借口。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人就是这样，装得久了，就装得像了；装得太像、太久，不管事实怎样，自己倒是先信了。

4．未知永远存在

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

不是“反对问为什么”，而是“暂时不去问为什么”可能更划算。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我们要了解未知分为两种：一种是永远不能解决的，另一种是在可预见的未来也许能够解决的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一个相对有效的策略是：当有问题解决不了时，可以先把它记下来，然后继续前行。

5．现状无法马上摆脱

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人们往往会低估环境的巨大能量。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

完全是“顾头不顾腚”的“屁话”一句。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

从某种意义上理解，“逆境造就成功”、“磨难令人成熟”之类的话纯属胡说八道。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

显然，在顺境中更容易成功，而且很多磨难根本没有必要——这更可能是失败者对他们自己一生都未曾有机会体验的成功及成功者“意淫”式的猜想而已。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

快乐是一种本事。

6．与时间做朋友

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTYuMjUgOC44MzkxOUM2LjI0OTUxIDYuMzM5MTkgOC4yNzM4MSA1LjAyOTY2IDEwLjA1OTUgNS4wMjk2NkMxMS44NDUyIDUuMDI5NjYgMTMuNjMxIDYuNjk2MzMgMTMuNjMxIDguMTI0OUMxMy42MzEgOC40MzQ3MyAxMy42NzkzIDguOTYyMjkgMTMuNzc2MSA5LjcwNzU2QzEzLjgyNzQgMTAuMTAzIDEzLjU5MTUgMTAuNDc5MyAxMy4yMTMyIDEwLjYwNTRMMTIuNzk3NiAxMC43NDM5VjEwLjkwNjhDMTIuNzk3NiAxMi4wNjY5IDExLjk5OTUgMTMuMDc0NiAxMC44NzAyIDEzLjM0MDNMMTAuNzczOCAxMy4zNjNWMTQuNTUzNUM5LjA3NDEzIDE0LjY3MTMgNy44ODM2NSAxNC4yNzQ1IDcuMjAyMzggMTMuMzYzQzcuMjAyMzggMTIuMTEyIDYuODg0OTIgMTAuNjA0MSA2LjI1IDguODM5MTlaTTkuNTIzODEgMTIuMzczTDEwLjU4MzkgMTIuMTIzNUMxMS4xNDg2IDExLjk5MDcgMTEuNTQ3NiAxMS40ODY4IDExLjU0NzYgMTAuOTA2OFY5Ljg0M0wxMi40OTM3IDkuNTI3NjRDMTIuNDE4OCA4LjkwNzM2IDEyLjM4MSA4LjQ0NjcgMTIuMzgxIDguMTI0OUMxMi4zODEgNy4zODE5NCAxMS4xNDA5IDYuMjc5NjYgMTAuMDU5NSA2LjI3OTY2QzguNzI0OSA2LjI3OTY2IDcuNjAwOTMgNy4yMTUyNSA3LjUwNjQzIDguNjQyMzVDOC4wNTcxOSAxMC4yMTk1IDguMzcwMjYgMTEuNjIyMiA4LjQzODI1IDEyLjg1ODlDOC42OTU5NCAxMy4wNjk0IDkuMDUyMDIgMTMuMjEzNCA5LjUyMzgxIDEzLjI4MDhWMTIuMzczWk0xMS45NjI0IDE0LjI3MDZDMTEuOTkyNSAxNC42MTQ1IDEyLjI5NTcgMTQuODY4OSAxMi42Mzk1IDE0LjgzODhDMTMuOTAwNCAxNC43Mjg1IDE0LjgzMyAxMy42MTY5IDE0LjcyMjcgMTIuMzU2MUMxNC42OTI3IDEyLjAxMjIgMTQuMzg5NSAxMS43NTc5IDE0LjA0NTYgMTEuNzg3OUMxMy43MDE4IDExLjgxOCAxMy40NDc0IDEyLjEyMTIgMTMuNDc3NSAxMi40NjVDMTMuNTI3NiAxMy4wMzgxIDEzLjEwMzcgMTMuNTQzNCAxMi41MzA2IDEzLjU5MzVDMTIuMTg2NyAxMy42MjM2IDExLjkzMjMgMTMuOTI2OCAxMS45NjI0IDE0LjI3MDZaIiBmaWxsPSIjOTlBMEFBIi8+Cjwvc3ZnPgo=)

不对，应该是：“在正确的时间，用正确的方式，做正确的事。”

与时间做朋友的方法很简单：用正确的方法做正确的事情。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

与时间做朋友的方法很简单：用正确的方法做正确的事情。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

怎样判断所做的事情是否正确？核心只有一个：看它是否现实。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

几乎一切愚蠢的行为都来自否定现实、逃避现实。只有接受现实，才可能脚踏实地，避免心浮气躁、好高骛远。如果我们把成功朴素地定义为“用正确的方法做正确的事情，并在最后期限之前漂亮地完成”的话

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

把“不均匀”理解成“不公平”，就可以理直气壮地打着“公平正义”的旗号为所欲为。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

明确经济学的根本目的——研究“如何运用有限的资源发挥最大的效用”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

以上提到的种种现实，包括“速成绝无可能”、“只有付出才有收获”、“完美永不存在”、“未知永远存在”、“现状无法马上摆脱”，都既清楚又简单，你必须要接受——不仅要接受，还要牢记；不仅要牢记，还要坚信，不容半点动摇。

1．估算时间

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

侯世达法则[插图]值得牢记：完成一个任务实际花费的时间总会超过计划花费的时间，就算制定计划的时候考虑到本法则，也不能避免这种情况的发生。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

为什么人们总是错误估计完成任务所需要的时间呢？因为大多数人在执行任务之前忽略了一个重要的步骤，那就是分辨任务的属性——它是熟悉的还是陌生的？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

对学习来说，任务“陌生”的可能性更大，因为学习本身是一个探索未知的过程。完成学习任务常常需要花费比我们想象中多得多的时间。对工作来说，任务“熟悉”的可能性更大。因为工作本身是一个应用已知的过程。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

想要出类拔萃，就要努力至少10000小时。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

做任何事情之前先判断其熟悉程度（或陌生程度），再据此判断估算完成任务所需要的时间。

2．及时行动

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

比“越早开始越好”更切实的答案是“现在就开始”。所谓做事拖延，不是拖延着做事，而是拖延着不开始做事

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

只要做事，就一定会出问题。这是现实——无论何人，无论何事。如果在做事的过程中没有出现任何问题，那肯定不是在做事，而是在做梦。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

做事情的时候，肯定会遇到困难，事情越有价值，困难就越具规模。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

—勤能补拙

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人是一种很有趣的动物，在自己做对、做好之前，通常已经了解做对、做好是什么样子。于是，无论能否做对、做好，人都觉得自己有能力判断别人是否做对、做好。所以，尽管自己不怎么样，却可以振振有词、理直气壮地评价别人做得对不对、好不好。这样看来，一个人一旦开始认真做事，被嘲弄、被耻笑的几率将远远高于被夸奖、被鼓励的几率——这几乎是肯定的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“不求有功，但求无过

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

事实上，那些真正能够做对、做好的人，绝不会随意嘲弄、打击别人，因为他们是做对过、做好过的人，他们一路走过来，心里非常清楚做对、做好有多么不易，所以，他们会不吝一切机会去鼓励那些尝试做事情的人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

尽管那些能真正做对、做好的人有时也会给出负面评价，但这些评价通常是“建设性的负面评价”，并不是为了获得优越感而发出的嘲弄。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所以，我们没有必要在意来自他人的、非建设性的负面评价。没有谁从一开始就能做对、做好。所有做对、做好的人都是一路磕磕绊绊走过来的，这就是生活常态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

而动辄给出非建设性负面评价的人，往往不是正经做事的人，他们和那些正经做事的人身处不一样的世界，这也是生活常态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在这样的情况下，唯一的策略依然是“现在就开始”——否则更待何时？在起步晚了的情况下，问题不是“到时候能不能做好”，而是“到时候能做多好就做多好，总好过什么都不做”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

永远不要再问“什么时候开始才好”，因为答案只有一个：现在！

3．直面困难

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

就算没有低估完成任务所需要的时间，就算已经迅速开始执行任务，很多人还是没有按时完成任务。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

为什么有的人好像一直在忙，却总是拿不出成绩、做不出成效？其实，工作中经常会遇到这样的人，读书的时候也不例外——上学时总有一些天天笔不离手，眼不离书，屁股不离板凳，成绩却很差的学生。这种情况的存在往往会使人们不禁怀疑“努力”的可靠性。还好，仔细观察就会发现，他们实际上并不努力，只是做出了努力的样子，或者显得比较努力而已。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

而效率低下的根本原因是什么？答案是：回避困难。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

任何一个任务都可以划分为两个部分，即相对简单的部分和相对困难的部分。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

合理的时间安排应该是这样的：迅速做完简单的部分，把节省出来的时间放在困难部分的处理上。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人做事的动机往往来自两个截然相反的原因：奖励与惩罚。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

接受惩罚往往是积累经验的起点，甚至是唯一的起点。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

受到奖励之后，原本有两个选项：“再次来过”和“见好就收”。有意思的是，绝大多数人会自动忽视第二个选项（这也是庞兹骗局[插图]生生不息的根本原因）。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

受到惩罚之后，同样有两个选项：“从此碰都不碰那件事情”和“挣扎着找一个出路”。同样有意思的是，绝大多数人还是会自动忽视第二个选项。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

他们做事，甚至做很多事。拖延的人也并非不努力——他们会花很长时间去做事，但做的只是很多简单的事。他们每次回避困难的时候，都不是故意的，并且往往已经给自己找了恰当的借口。这借口太强大、太有力，以至他们真诚地相信：“我喜欢做有创意的事情，而现在手上的这些事情太枯燥，我确实提不起兴趣……”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

现实中，这种现象无处不在。例如学习上，准备托福考试时只做阅读和听力但不练习口语和写作；例如工作上，做项目计划时只讨论做什么却从不提及怎么做；例如生活上，总是把“我爱你”挂在嘴边却从来不花时间想想恋人真正需要的是什么……这些问题都源自同一个习惯：专做简单的，回避困难的。

4．关注步骤

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所谓“三思而行”在我看来就是指做任何事情之前都要考虑相关的3个方面：内容（What）、原因（Why）、方法（How）

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

大多数人都知道自己究竟想要得到什么，也知道为什么要得到，却始终没弄明白怎样做才能得到。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

面对的任务的“内容”就比较具体了。但是，还可以再具体一点：扩充词汇量→托福词汇→托福核心词汇→21个单元→每个单元大约100个单词→一个单元分2次完成……

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在这个过程中，对任务的每一次“具体化”与“细分拆解”都要反复询问“原因”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

有了这样的结果，就可以开始思考“方法”了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

假设这位学生根据自己的情况，已经决定将“一个单元分2次完成”，也就是说，21乘以2，总计42个阶段。那么，在这42个阶段里他应该具体如何操作呢？● 先尝试做一两个阶段，测量一下完成1个阶段需要多长时间。● 按照测量的结果制作一个时间表，把其余阶段所需要的时间填写完整（最终总是需要做一些调整的）。● 背单词需要重复，所以，每3个阶段过后要留出与完成1个阶段相等的时间去复习。这就意味着一共需要花费完成56（42+14）个阶段的时间。● 每完成总任务的1/3，就增加与完成1个阶段相等的再复习时间。这就意味着一共需要花费完成59（56+3）个阶段的时间。● 学习过程中可能需要多次快速重复记忆，每次可能相当于完成3～5个阶段所需要的时间。由于熟悉程度的不断增加，每次重复记忆所需要的时间会越来越短，所以，预计进行3次重复记忆需要相当于完成10个阶段的时间。这就意味着一共需要花费完成69（59+10）个阶段的时间。作出以上规划后，还要认真思考完成每个阶段的具体步骤。当然，越具体越好。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

每天早晨腾出一点时间。● 把前一天背过的单词朗读至少2遍。● 听录音，跟读当天要背的单词3～5遍，主要关注发音、拼写，顺带看看词义，能记多少就记多少，不求速成。● 上午利用闲暇时间通读词汇列表，并反复阅读例句。● 下午用专门的时间把当天要背的单词集中背2～3遍。可以一边读，一边抄，一边背，不要只是坐在那里呆呆地盯着词汇看。● 空闲时反复听当天要背的单词，重复次数越多越好。● 晚上睡觉前复习当天背的单词。有了这种思考，随后的一切行动会因此变得相当容易。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在做任何事情之前，通过关注“方法”去反复拆分任务，最终确认每个子任务都是可完成的，这是一个人不可或缺的功课。这样的习惯，会使一个人变得现实、踏实。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这既是一种习惯，也是一种后天习得的技能。这种技能无比重要，却常常被忽视，因为掌握这种技能的人总是默默地应用它，而忽视这种技能的人从未看到过它的具体实施过程和巨大好处。

5．并行串行

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一般情况下，“提高效率”指的就是“原本只能串行完成的两个任务现在可以并行完成”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

养成一个习惯——把要做的事情用纸和笔写下来，把任务落到纸面上，就可以比较容易地分辨出哪些任务是简单而又机械的，哪些任务是相对复杂而又灵活的（对我个人来讲，需要思考的就是“非机械”的），然后，尝试把一个非机械的任务和一个机械的任务搭配起来完成。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

并行两个任务的一个重要前提是执行者足够了解这两个任务，且对自己有足够清楚的认识，即，对执行者来说，这两个任务是“主动并行”的。被动发生的并行任务往往只能使效率变得更为低下。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

让自己拥有“多任务操作系统”的另一个方法就是切分自己的时间。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

而多任务操作系统把一个长时间段划分成很多短小的时间片，每个时间片只让处理器执行一个进程[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在这个机制里，进程不是按其本质属性被划分为子进程，而是被处理器的时间片硬性划分为进程片。这是关键。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

因其他人的错误而耽误自己的时间。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

把自己的时间切分成“时间片”[插图]

6．感知时间

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

基于过程的记录，不仅更详尽，还有另外一个巨大的好处——结果不好的时候更容易找到缘由。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

想明白“基于过程的”与“基于结果的”两种记录之间的区别之后，我开始尝试着在自己记录的每个事件后面加上时间。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我就体会到这种新的记录方法的另一个巨大好处：它会使你对时间的感觉越来越精确。前

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

既然管理时间是不可能的，那么解决方法就只能是：想尽一切办法真正了解自己、真正了解时间、精确感知时间，而后再想尽一切办法使自己及自己的行为与时间“合拍”。按我的话说就是——“与时间做朋友”。

8．制订预算

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

前面的练习可以帮助我们养成一个好习惯：每天记录时间开销。如果这个习惯已经养成，我们还要养成第二个好习惯：每天制订时间预算。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在罗列这些任务的时候，你的大脑就要自动开始估算完成每项任务究竟要花费多少时间了。很快，你就会遇到第一个问题：任务太多，无法全部完成。于是，你只好进行选择。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

解决这个问题的方法倒也简单，就是给列表中的每项任务标上权重[插图]，

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

实际上，我认为对大多数人来讲，用数字1～3已经足够，因为这种设计基本上可以代表：● 不重要● 一般● 重要

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

考虑之后，我们需要重新审视一下已经被标注为“重要”的那些任务，因为其中必然有一些只不过是“显得重要”而已。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

判断一项任务是否“真的重要”其实只需要一个标准：这项任务的完成是否确实对达成目标有益。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

无用的事情，哪怕非常有趣，都不应该去做；而有用的事情，哪怕非常无趣，都应该去做。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

现在就开始把自己的那些哪怕不切实际的目标作为标准来判断吧——判断每项任务的真实属性，然后选择“真的重要的”或者“显得不重要的”。

9．计划

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

计划成功的前提：目标现实可行

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

有了目标，就可以倒推每个实施步骤，最终自然地形成计划。所有真正执行到底的计划，都是因为其目标现实可行。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

他生气不是因为我说了实话，而是因为没听到他想要听到的话。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

证明我的目标现实可行的方法比较简单：● 已经有人做到了。● 我与那个人没有太大的差距。对这两个简单的衡量标准，也需要多少做些说明。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“已经有人做到了”，并不代表我也能做到。他用多长时间做到的？他通过什么方式做到的？我和他的区别究竟在什么地方？哪些是我确实无法超越的？我的相对优势在哪里？我有没有可能通过一些方式弥补我的相对缺陷？也许还要问更多的问题，才能够确定我们的目标确实是现实并且可行的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果发现既定的目标确实是不现实、不可行的，那么“半途而废”不仅不意味着失败，反而意味着决策者的无比理智。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

长期计划是需要通过实践才能习得的能力

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

计划总是被变化打乱的深层次的原因在于：计划过于长远。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

做长期计划显然是正确并且必需的，但是，并非每个人都有制定长期计划的能力。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

计划固然重要，行动更为重要。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

有些时候没必要做计划，原因只是任务非常简单。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

综上所述，没必要做计划的原因主要有两个，除了前面提到过的“任务其实非常简单”之外，另一个原因是“初始状态下，我们往往并没有能力去制定合理有效的计划”。
