![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

对那些渴望成功而又尚未成功的人来说，成功人士“苦大仇深”、“血泪斑斑”的经历是一种多大的安慰啊！

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人类大脑具有的一个自我保护功能——遗忘痛苦。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

有些时候，“成功者”的经验没什么用，因为那些经验根本就是错误的，而这一点“成功者”自己可能也不了解。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

例如，他们遇到了一个经济飞速增长的时代，无论做什么都赚钱，并且赚得很多，所以从宏观上来看，根本就不是他们自己所认为的宝贵经验在起作用，而是宏观经济给了他们这样的机会。但是，有谁愿意承认自己的成功跟自己的经验没有关系呢？人类普遍拥有的一个认知偏差就是：把成功揽到自己身上，把失败归咎于别人或者坏运气。这在心理学上有个术语——自利性偏差[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

那些“成功者”这么做的时候往往并不是有意欺骗——他们甚至出于好意。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要知道，有些“宝贵经验”即使正确，放到别人身上也可能并不那么灵验。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

最可能让一个人误入歧途的，就是他对自己的了解。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

成功者们常说，他们并不在意钱，他们知道人格的可贵。但是，大部分听众和他们不一样。大部分听众现在没有足够的钱！相信我，绝大多数人，在没有钱的时候，对“人格可贵”的理解很难非常深刻。人活着是要吃饭的，一个人的家眷是不应该被饿着的，在基本条件都不能保障的时候，“人格有个屁用”就成了很多人的选择。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这是大实话，而大实话往往不可能动听。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这并不是玩世不恭或者愤世嫉俗的说法，只是有勇气接受现实的人对生活的平静描述。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

与其关注成功者，不妨反其道而行之——努力从失败者身上汲取经验。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

。不过，观察失败者却相对容易得多，因为失败者的失败往往是明显的、确定的，失败的真正原因也往往很容易查实（尽管失败者会找各种各样的借口）。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“幸运”——当你马上就要犯错误的时候，有人先犯了同样的错误。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人家说什么你就信什么，挺傻的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

只有经过自己的仔细分辨，真正成功者的宝贵经验才是无价的。需要额外注意的是，一方面要多花心思分辨，另一方面要多花时间真正了解自己，以便能够避开“一概而论、生搬硬套”可能带来的灾难。

10．克服恐惧

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

日常生活中，那些原本是讨论者，后来却变成了“为争而争”的争辩者，常常并非故意。他们只是像醒过来后最终还是要咬农夫的蛇一样，展现出了他们难移的本性而已。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所有这些最终都可以归结于人性中根深蒂固的恐惧和恐惧带来的懦弱。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人们总是喜欢用善恶区分一切，但这其实是一件很无聊的事情，没有什么实际意义。更有意义的区分是“强”与“弱”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“强”与“弱”才是自然界中真正存在的本质，“善”与“恶”往往只是弱者一厢情愿的定义。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

成功者害怕自己的既得利益受到损害，于是在“分享”成功经验时着了魔一样地夸大自己遇到的各种障碍，同时却对起着决定性作用的“运气”绝口不提

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人人都有弱点，因为人人都会有恐惧。恐惧需要克服，勇气需要培养。事实上，“勇气需要培养”这句话里面的“培养”不如换成一个更朴素的词——积累。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

当一个人只有一点点勇气的时候，就期望他可以“除暴安良”、“替天行道”、“匡扶正义”是非常幼稚且不现实的想法。一个人的强与弱，实际上就相当于他的勇气减去他的恐惧之后的分值——如果是正数，那么他是强的；如果是负数，那么他是弱的。所有人的起点都是负数。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

古人说，人贵自知。摆脱“自以为是”陷阱的一个重要前提就是正视自己的恐惧，因为恐惧永远存在。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所以，我们有什么理由不能理解别人的恐惧呢？

11．辅助工具

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

其实不说脏话的人不一定不‘脏’；偶尔说点脏话有助心理健康

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

……本来（原本）就是嘛！

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这种句式在生活中只有一个用处——找（最后的）借口。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

永远不要再跟我说“我认为……”了！你的看法关我屁事？我要的是事实……

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

那个毛头小伙就刻意让自己写的句子都用“事实上”作为开头，而为了配得上这个开头，在后面的陈述中，他真的不知不觉地剔除了很多“偏见”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

原来在很多领域，有些“思维训练”其实只是需要更改语言习惯。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

● ……是一回事，而……是另外一回事。● ……和……其实根本不是一回事。● ……不一定……● ……可是，这并不意味着……● ……也许还有另外一种可能性（解释）。● ……看起来像……可是……● ……而事实却可能远比看起来的更为复杂（简单）。● ……然而，（这个论断）反过来（陈述）却不一定成立，因为……● ……其实很可能与……根本就没有任何关系。● ……和……之间不一定是单纯的因果关系，它们也可能互为因果。● ……和……之间的比较也许没有任何意义。● ……其实不过是表面现象，其背后的本质是……● ……有一个通常被忽略的前提。● ……尽管听起来很有道理，然而却完全不现实。● ……也许有人会说……但是这种质疑却……

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

而另外一些句式，则要刻意回避。例如这句话：……难道就没有一点可取之处吗？当我们试图批判一个错误立场的时候，即便是在完全正确地批判的情况下，也总是会遇到这样的抵抗（往往来自那些不知其所以然的所谓“同情者”）：“……难道就没有一点可取之处吗？”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

很多人分不清“自己的观点被批评”与“自己被批评”之间的重大差异

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要是“……还是有一些可取之处”可以成为我们必须拥护，或者不得反对某个立场或观点的可成立的理由的话，我们就几乎必须拥护所有立场、不得反对任何立场了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

但仅仅因为它也有一些可取之处就不能批判它，就一定要拥护它，或者反过来说，就可以纵容它去误导更多的人吗？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这个常见的句子还有一个变体：“我发现……还是很有一些道理的！”唉，那不是废话吗？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“我发现……还是很有一些道理的！”常常成为很多人把垃圾当宝贝的唯一理由。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

垃圾里当然也可能有些宝贝，但是在宝贝已在眼前、用都用不完的时候，为什么还一定要跑到臭气熏天的垃圾堆里“淘宝”呢？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

再看一个最浪费时间的，也因此必须回避的句型：“要是……就好了！”这个句型是用来表达后悔情绪的，而“后悔”是最浪费时间的——无论如何，这种情绪都于事无补。当

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

过去的事情是无法更改的，现在的烦恼是无济于事的，但是将来的尴尬也许是可以避免的——如果现在的行动没有出错的话。换句话讲，为了避免将来的尴尬，必须在今天采取正确的行动。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

，“要是……就好了！”这种念头不仅无益，甚至可能是有害的，因为这个句型会衍生出一个很恐怖的句型：“要是……就好了！但……”

1．学会倾听

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

。从某种意义上讲，交流的有效与否往往更取决于听者而非说者，反过来说，失败的交流往往源自听者的疏忽。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

另外，说者为了讲解清楚来龙去脉，往往不得不把重要的信息，如重要的事实、迂回的说理、意味深远的结论，放在后面。从总体上来看，说者发出的信息越来越重要，可是听者接收的信息却越来越少、越来越零散。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

：人们只能听到自己想听到的，只能看到自己想看到的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人类就是不喜欢不直观的东西，因为不喜欢，自然就不接受

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在了解“应该做什么”之前，有必要先了解一下“最不应该做的是什么”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

为了真正做到有效倾听，最需要克制的就是“过早质疑”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

不成熟的人、思维简单的人更倾向于频繁地插话，并且他们总是认为“我已经了解你要说什么了……

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“过早质疑”同样会造成幻觉——觉得对方的论证不堪一击。可事实总是与此相反。道理很简单，讲者刚刚开始自己的论述时，驳斥他的难度是最低的，于是“过早质疑”的人总会产生自以为是的幻觉，进而落入自己设置的陷阱，同时自我感觉良好。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“过早质疑”的另一个副作用是它会让听者不由自主地进入排斥状态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

大多数人在未经训练的情况下，在听的过程中只有两种状态——接收和排斥。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

为了让自己听得更有效率，我们要牢牢记住这个简单而又实用的原则：就算需要质疑，也一定要等到对方把话说完。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在倾听的过程中，我们可以利用多余的脑力处理两个方向的信息：“回顾”与“预期”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

说者刚刚都讲了些什么？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

只有相信这个事实，才能够在倾听的时候有意识地为了真正记住而反复（认真）回顾。在一些重要场合（课堂、会议等），也会因此真诚地借助辅助工具（笔记、照片、录音等）来帮助记忆。很

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

准确地讲，那些隐含的信息不是“听”到的，而是“想”到的——动用自己“多余”的脑力想到的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

说者的语篇内容可以分为两类：事实和看法。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTYuMjUgOC44MzkxOUM2LjI0OTUxIDYuMzM5MTkgOC4yNzM4MSA1LjAyOTY2IDEwLjA1OTUgNS4wMjk2NkMxMS44NDUyIDUuMDI5NjYgMTMuNjMxIDYuNjk2MzMgMTMuNjMxIDguMTI0OUMxMy42MzEgOC40MzQ3MyAxMy42NzkzIDguOTYyMjkgMTMuNzc2MSA5LjcwNzU2QzEzLjgyNzQgMTAuMTAzIDEzLjU5MTUgMTAuNDc5MyAxMy4yMTMyIDEwLjYwNTRMMTIuNzk3NiAxMC43NDM5VjEwLjkwNjhDMTIuNzk3NiAxMi4wNjY5IDExLjk5OTUgMTMuMDc0NiAxMC44NzAyIDEzLjM0MDNMMTAuNzczOCAxMy4zNjNWMTQuNTUzNUM5LjA3NDEzIDE0LjY3MTMgNy44ODM2NSAxNC4yNzQ1IDcuMjAyMzggMTMuMzYzQzcuMjAyMzggMTIuMTEyIDYuODg0OTIgMTAuNjA0MSA2LjI1IDguODM5MTlaTTkuNTIzODEgMTIuMzczTDEwLjU4MzkgMTIuMTIzNUMxMS4xNDg2IDExLjk5MDcgMTEuNTQ3NiAxMS40ODY4IDExLjU0NzYgMTAuOTA2OFY5Ljg0M0wxMi40OTM3IDkuNTI3NjRDMTIuNDE4OCA4LjkwNzM2IDEyLjM4MSA4LjQ0NjcgMTIuMzgxIDguMTI0OUMxMi4zODEgNy4zODE5NCAxMS4xNDA5IDYuMjc5NjYgMTAuMDU5NSA2LjI3OTY2QzguNzI0OSA2LjI3OTY2IDcuNjAwOTMgNy4yMTUyNSA3LjUwNjQzIDguNjQyMzVDOC4wNTcxOSAxMC4yMTk1IDguMzcwMjYgMTEuNjIyMiA4LjQzODI1IDEyLjg1ODlDOC42OTU5NCAxMy4wNjk0IDkuMDUyMDIgMTMuMjEzNCA5LjUyMzgxIDEzLjI4MDhWMTIuMzczWk0xMS45NjI0IDE0LjI3MDZDMTEuOTkyNSAxNC42MTQ1IDEyLjI5NTcgMTQuODY4OSAxMi42Mzk1IDE0LjgzODhDMTMuOTAwNCAxNC43Mjg1IDE0LjgzMyAxMy42MTY5IDE0LjcyMjcgMTIuMzU2MUMxNC42OTI3IDEyLjAxMjIgMTQuMzg5NSAxMS43NTc5IDE0LjA0NTYgMTEuNzg3OUMxMy43MDE4IDExLjgxOCAxMy40NDc0IDEyLjEyMTIgMTMuNDc3NSAxMi40NjVDMTMuNTI3NiAxMy4wMzgxIDEzLjEwMzcgMTMuNTQzNCAxMi41MzA2IDEzLjU5MzVDMTIuMTg2NyAxMy42MjM2IDExLjkzMjMgMTMuOTI2OCAxMS45NjI0IDE0LjI3MDZaIiBmaWxsPSIjOTlBMEFBIi8+Cjwvc3ZnPgo=)

逻辑学

如果是事实，那么我们就要花时间想想“他所陈述的内容真实性如何”。如果是看法，那么我们就要花时间想想“他的这个看法/意见的根源在哪”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果是事实，那么我们就要花时间想想“他所陈述的内容真实性如何”。如果是看法，那么我们就要花时间想想“他的这个看法/意见的根源在哪”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果能够记住要点，并肯花时间和精力搜寻隐含的信息，听者便有能力去做下一件更重要的事情：预期。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

最后，我们还要养成一个重要的习惯：一旦决定倾听，就要主动帮助说者进入“倾诉”状态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

不过，作为听者，尤其是能被说者看到的听者，给予说者鼓励性的信号会使说者更容易地进入“倾诉”状态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人们往往会因为讨厌内容而讨厌说者，或者反过来，因为讨厌说者而讨厌内容

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

适度控制自己的反感情绪对获取信息也会有极大的正面作用——既然坐在那里，“听而不闻”就是浪费自己的时间。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一旦听者决定倾听某人的话，就要想办法调动自己的所有感官去感受说者的一切表达方式，包括他的眼神、姿态、动作等，随时随刻尽可能地去想象说者正在经历的情绪状态。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

那些善于沟通的人往往在恰当的时候使用这样的句式：“那你看我这么理解对不对……”说者这时会自然而然地想尽一切办法表述清楚，甚至会在这个过程中突然发觉自己的疏忽之处，进而没有压力地进行自我纠正。

2．说与不说

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

明明是同样的话，自己说出来就不像那么回事。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

每一句话，其实都是有归属的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在更细微的地方，这种归属造成的扭曲感会更严重。例如，若不是班里学习最好的学生在大讲特讲学习方法，很多同学会不屑于听。再如，若某个人不是公认最冷静、最善于思考的人，那么他说出来的话就算是对的，也很可能会被低估。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

得知道什么话能说，什么话不能说。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要根据自己的情况选择能说的话、该说的话、说出来别人能听的话。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

通过努力、通过积累成为能说更多话的人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

尊重只能靠积累获得，这是铁律。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

有时，我们知道自己说的是对的，可还是没有人听得进去。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

可事实上，这往往只说明一个问题——还没有赢得足够的重视。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

对很多人来说，“知无不言，言无不尽[插图]”在大部分情况下是最浪费时间和精力的做法[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

当一个人不被认为是“能说那话的人”时，一般不大可能“百人誉之”，不是“百人毁之”就很好了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

分辨谈话的对象

3．交流守则

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

第一个原则：有意义的讨论的前提是双方不仅要“相互竞争”，更要“相互合作”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

因为讲道理是需要前提的。双方想要进行有意义的讨论，最基本的要求就是双方必须共同遵守“理性讨论基本原则[插图]”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果我们作为讨论的一方，发现对方已经不再“遵守理性讨论基本原则”，那么就马上停止讨论吧，

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

第二个原则：真理是独立存在的，它从来不会依附于任何个人或者集体

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果我们在任何讨论中发现参与者里面有“自以为是”者存在，那么最好的选择只有一个——退出讨论。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

，只要他们存在，讨论就不再是讨论，也不会得出任何有意义的结果，继续下去只会浪费自己的时间。而我们千万不要自以为是到认为自己有能力、有时间、有责任、有义务教会他们“想明白”的本领，甚至带他们跨越那道阻挡大多数人的障碍，这任务几近不可能完成。首先，在绝大多数情况下，心智成长都是自己的事情，并且只是自己的事情；其次，这是几乎每个社会都想系统地完成却从来没有成功完成的事情（因为每个社会中总是存在着另外一股强大的阻挠力量）；最后，我们也应该考虑自身的安全，即不要被“吸血鬼”咬到，甚至最好不要被他们看到。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

第三个原则：真理不变，也不会因任何人而变；不停变化的只是人们对真理的解释或理解

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我们在讨论（甚至争论）的时候，原本的焦点在于“事实”，而非“看法”，因为“看法”无法争论——“看法”只是对事实的“理解”而已

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

事实上，如果交流从一开始就以“看法”为焦点，那么就没必要讨论甚至争论了

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“每个人都有自己的看法”这句话却是非常扯淡的——对很多人来说，那看法究竟是不是他的，他自己也不知道。大多数人根本不思考，而少数肯思考的人的大部分又不懂得应该如何思考，所以，绝大多数人只不过是环境的产物而已。很多时候，所谓的“主流”观点并非因为“正确”才成为“主流”，而是因为它恰好适合（或者迎合）那些不善思考、不愿思考的人的感觉。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

大多数人的大多数看法，基本上都是被灌输的，只不过对他们来说，那些“想当然”的看法早已与他们共生多年，不分你我。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

心智成长是自己的事情

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

是做快乐的猪，还是痛苦的苏格拉底[插图]？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

正如没有人能帮得上你一样，估计你也帮不上别人。你可以为之努力，就好像我现在做的这样，但，效果如何，不在于你。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

很多时候，好的意图不一定会带来好的结果……

4．正确复述

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我们的“解码”结果不见得正确。所以，为了保证沟通顺利，往往需要添加一个验证机制，或者说反馈机制。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“你的意思是……是吗？”或者“你的意思是……我理解得对吗？”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

就算他只是出于无心，也相当难办，因为我们没义务，更重要的是估计也没能力去改变他。

5．勤于反思

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

事实上，每个人都有来自各个方向的局限，例如认知上的、经验上的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

摆脱经验主义的第一个技巧就是“了解经验的局限”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

使用记录，使自己能够记住更多经验做记录是一个很好的习惯。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

观察和阅读，是扩充有限的自我经验的最好手段。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

每个人每时每刻都有观察的机会，但绝大多数人仅仅因为自己的态度问题就失去了积累、成长的可能。要解决这个态度问题，只需要在平时多琢磨一下“他们为什么那么想？”“他们为什么那么做？”“他们为什么那么看？”避免用“傻屄！”来评价那些与自己的想法、做法、看法不一样的人，就可以了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

类比思考几乎是跨越已知与未知之间鸿沟的唯一手段。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

遇到不理解的问题，遇到不确定的想法，最好马上记录下来。不一定非要急着获得答案——马上获得解答往往是不可能的。

1．兴趣

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

不是对自己正在做的事情没有兴趣，而是没有能力把目前正在做的事情做好。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

几乎没有人会喜欢做自己做不好的事情，每个人都会不自觉地尽量回避自己的短处

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我不喜欢做某件事情，是不是仅仅因为这件事我没有做好？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

若是因为自己没有做好而不喜欢，就要考虑另一个问题：做好这件事情究竟对我有没有意义？

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果有，那就努力做，直到做好为止，没有其他选择。反过来，自己做得挺好，但就是不喜欢，纯粹因为那件事对自己确实没有什么吸引力——事实上这种情况少之又少——直接换一件事情做吧。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

其次，人们总说他们真正感兴趣的是其他事情。可事实上，出现这种感觉应该仅仅是因为还没有开始做那件事情，也还没有在那件事情上遭受挫折而已。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

，兴趣并不是很重要，至少没有我们想象得那么重要。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

某件事情只要能做好，并且做到比大多数人好，他就不会对那件事情没兴趣。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

根据孩子的情况，选出孩子最可能做得比别人好的事情（这很可能已经是极其耗时费力的了）

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

然后绞尽脑汁让孩子学得会、做得好、做得比一般人好、做得比谁都好——兴趣就自然出现了。
