于是，甲所拥有的非常优秀的那些方面——假设可以打99分（100分制，下同）——相对于他所拥有的水平一般的那些方面——65分——差距太大——高达34分。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

而另外一个没那么优秀的人（姑且称他为“乙”）所拥有的还算优秀的那些方面——80分——相对于他所拥有的那些水平一般的方面——60分——差距仅有20分。这样一来，从自我满意度的角度来看，优秀的甲要比平凡的乙承受更大的落差。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

甲明显会感受更多的痛苦——尽管他实际上无论在哪个方面都比乙优秀。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

从这个角度出发，反倒是那些资质在各方面都处于平均水平的人更不容易自卑。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

差到极致的难度绝不亚于好到极致的难度。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

自信和自卑的衡量标准是在自己身上，还是要以别人为参照物呢？事实上，既不该在自己身上，也不该以别人为参照物。美与丑的分别、强与弱的不同、慧与痴的差异，并不依附个人观点而存在，也不会因为任何人的看法而改变。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

想做到“不以物喜，不以己悲”的健康状态，要迈出的第一步就是——停止嘲弄他人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

生活中我们很少真的遇到他人的“弱”影响了我们的“强”的情况。嘲弄别人“弱”往往只是为了证明自己的“强”，而真的“强”是不需要证明的，需要证明的“强”其实是清楚自证的“弱”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

嘲弄者必被嘲弄

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

另一个比较“技术”一点的手段是“忘记自己的优点”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

那些“如何克服缺点”的说辞不仅愚蠢，而且可笑。其实，更准确地说，克服自卑只需要“尽量漠视自己的优点”就好了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在一个“自卑”、“自信”、“自负”几乎全部被扭曲定义的社会里，一个人“尽量漠视自己的优点”带来的最直接的好处就是他会被赞誉淹没，因为他太“谦虚”、太“低调”了。其实，他也没做什么，只是做了一件所有成熟的人都善于去做的事情——让别人舒服。很多时候，所谓“谦虚”和“低调”其实是一种自我保护的优化策略。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

还有一个相当不错的手段，是我的一位朋友告诉我的。她的方法是：在自己的语言中，把“优点”和“缺点”这两个词替换成“特点”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

因为用“特点”这个中性词取代“优点”、“缺点”这种明显带有褒贬含义的词，她就能很容易地做到平静对待自己的各种特点，也平静对待他人的各种特点了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人们口中的“优点”和“缺点”往往是相对的

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

最后一个方法是“适当地放纵一下自己”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

承认自己是一个有缺点的人，是让心智获得解放的重要前提。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

“自卑”一下能怎么样？“自负”一下能怎么样？“虚荣”一下又能怎么样？如果仅仅因为一个人“自卑”了一下、“自负”了一下或者“虚荣”了一下，他身边的人就受伤了，那么有问题的其实不是他，是他身边的人——他们太脆弱了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所有的方法都需要花上一点时间和精力才能正确操作。拿出一张纸、一支笔，罗列一下吧。在左边罗列你的优点，在右边罗列你的缺点——花上一天时间也不过分，因为我们需要分辨“这个真的是我的优点吗”和“这个真的是我的缺点吗”。完成这一步后，再试着猜想一下别人是如何看待我们的优点或者缺点的。我们甚至可以旁敲侧击去了解一下—

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

自己的缺点当中有没有可能会给其他人造成伤害的？如果有，请想办法克服。每个人都一定会有一些“无伤大雅的缺点”，适当地在这些方面放纵一下吧，相信我，这种“适当的放纵”对我们克服那些“可能会给其他人造成伤害的缺点”有巨大的帮助。

8．灵感

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

博学”背后的真相是——有意识地积累！

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人类大脑中的灰质所储存的各种信息里只有很少的一部分（很难超过12%）是有序存储的，这些部分被人们称作“有意识”的。而更多的信息或者信息碎片是无序储存的，甚至是很难通过意识直接调出的，这些部分往往被人们称作“无意识”或者“潜意识”的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

随着信息输入量的增加，大脑会因为需要而主动生成新的灰质细胞。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

科学家们已经发现，使用两种或者两种以上语言的人的大脑拥有更多的灰质细胞。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

所有的成功，本质上都是一样的。先花上相当的时间和精力去锁定一个方向或者目标。确定它现实可行之后，运用心智的力量，在这个方向上投入更多的时间，比更多再多一点的时间。把时间当作朋友，一路前行。当时间陪伴你足够久的时候，它自会给你的耐心相应的回报。

9．鼓励

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

永远鼓励身边的人，哪怕多少有些盲目。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

终于有一天，我发现，大多数人是以“泼冷水”为乐的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

他们原本跟我一样——他们也“跟大多数人不一样[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

尽管他们不见得希望你跟他们一样，但他们一定不喜欢你跟他们不一样。他们心里想说的是：“凭什么呀？”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

当我们不停地鼓励所有人的时候，最大的受益者其实是我们自己，因为最终我们会发现，自己开始进入一种他人无法想象的状态，成为一个不需要他人鼓励的人。

10．效率

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

没有任何机器可以一直用100%的功率运转，人也一样。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果一个人强迫自己一定要如此，那么他必然会像那些始终用100%的功率运转的机器一样，由于损耗太大而提前报废。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

纯时间要比毛时间少得多。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在做时间预算的时候，一定要留有空间。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一个人除了工作、学习之外，一定要保证自己有足够的其他活动。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要做一个正常人——这是每个人的权利。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

一个正常人，每天都要做很多工作和学习之外的事情，例如：喝点茶或者喝点咖啡，甚至有些人是必须喝点酒的；读读报，翻翻闲书，当然，更多的人喜欢看看电视或者电影；散散步，爬爬山，还有一些人会很规律地去健身房确保自己的身体一切正常；男人看看姑娘、女人瞄瞄帅哥，毫无疑问，对成年人来讲，保证规律而健康的两性交往，对心理健康很有帮助……

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果一个人把大部分的时间花在工作和学习上，那么他是以工作成就为导向的人；如果一个人把大部分的时间花在享受欢乐上，那么他是以生活满足为导向的人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

选择意味着放弃。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果一天你可以规划的时间有10小时，并且你确定自己是以工作成就为导向的人，那就这样规划吧：用大约6.18小时去工作和学习，而用剩下的大约3.82小时去享受欢乐——你毕竟是一个正常人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果你确定自己是以生活满足为导向的人，那就这样规划吧：用大约6.18小时去享受欢乐，而用剩下的大约3.82小时去工作和学习——你毕竟还要想办法养活自己。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

人本质上应该是“被自己的大脑所控制”的人，而不是“控制自己的大脑”的人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

看看每天自己做的事情里，有多少是尽管无趣却非常重要的，有多少是非常有趣却不重要的。如果我们一整天都在做那些非常重要但可能并无乐趣的事情，那就意味着，我们已经完全摆脱了大脑的控制，进而成为大脑的真正主人了。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

其实这世间的绝大多数事情都是一样的——不见得一定要做到极致才可以。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

因为61.8分以上的成绩，必须放弃很多才可以获得。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我常常觉得，很多快乐是建立在“自知之明”上的。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

平庸的人也有权利快乐。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

[插图]

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

请再次拿出纸和笔，罗列一下那些尽管无趣，但实际上对你来说非常重要的事情吧！

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

挑出一件你认为最重要的事情，然后给自己做个时间表，保证自己在未来的一个星期乃至一个月的时间里每天至少专注于这件事情2小时

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

实际上，我敢打赌，在自己不喜欢的事情上专注2小时，未经训练的你肯定做不到，

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

最初的时候，可以参考“番茄工作法[插图]”。例如，你需要专注于这件事情2小时，即120分钟，那你就可以把当天的任务分解成6块，每一块用20分钟去完成，再把20分钟当作专注的基本时间单位，在每个时间单位过后休息5分钟，想办法犒劳一下自己——喝杯喜欢的饮料，或者给恋人打个电话说点肉麻的话……在休息时间的最后1分钟，重新振作，试着恢复状态，进入下一个基本时间单位——另一个20分钟。

11．节奏

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

很多人的计划之所以无法坚持，是因为他们的计划实际上是“超人计划”

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

凡是值得做的事情，都值得慢慢去做，做很久很久。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

这也就解释了为什么有那么多的人总是幻想什么“速成”的方法——他们前期松懈了太久，突然发现时间不够了，最后期限马上就到了，所以只能寄希望于“速成”方法的存在。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

想办法提前预知自己需要掌握哪些技能，再确定它们是自己可以通过练习真正熟练掌握的技能，而后制定长期计划，一点一点稳步执行。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

切实懂得这样的道理之后，我们才会真正审视生活，然后开始醒悟。任何人一旦醒悟，再看身边忙忙碌碌却又庸庸无为的人，就会知道他们其实有多可笑了——他们一生都在追求实际上根本得不到的东西。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

要么对人生失望，要么选择某个宗教，而后寄希望于来世。

12．物极必反

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

创业者在其创业的过程中往往更在意“开源”，也常常因为如此而最终成功；后继的守业者却往往会把“节流”当作主要的工作内容，因为“开源”也许并不是他们所擅长的。然而，真正的成功者，在关注“开源”的时候，会并不吝惜金钱地合理“节流”；在关注“节流”的时候，也不会忘记“开源”的重要性。道理很简单：任何事都可能“物极必反”。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我把自己夜间的睡眠时间缩短到4小时；然后，在中午12点左右，想办法找个合适的地方打盹30分钟；到下午18点左右，再找个地方打盹30分钟。这样，我削减了3小时的睡眠时间，同样精力充沛。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在打盹之前喝一小杯咖啡，然后迅速睡过去。这样，在30分钟后醒来时，大脑就会处于清晰的状态，这种感觉真的很棒。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

尽量不要减少与家人交流的时间

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

但正因为你是成年人，你才应该想尽一切办法不让你的家人为你操心。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

为了在需要别人帮助的时候不碰壁，我们要学会不停地帮助身边的人。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

我们要想尽一切办法，运用自己的资源，为值得帮助的人提供帮助。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果在外地的朋友来电话求你帮忙去书店买本书并寄给他，那就一定要尽快——当然，你必须同时告诉他可能会有些耽搁。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

在决定是否给别人提供帮助的时候，要考虑他是否值得我们帮助。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

把值得自己帮助的人的特征都写下来，看看自己是否满足这些特征。如

13．自我证明

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

证明自己给别人看”恰恰是最浪费生命的一种行为。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果某个人出色，却仍然要刻意证明，可能招致不必要的麻烦，例如引来小人的嫉妒——天下最可怕的事情之一。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

其实这是人类大脑所拥有的自我保护功能。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

你比别人强一点根本没用，真正有用的是你比别人强很多很多。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

当你最终竟然在某一方面比别人强很多的时候会面临什么境遇？哈哈，可能会出乎你的意料——你身边的人不再在这方面跟你比了，他们会自动转向，跟你比你不如他们的地方！还

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

长久的观察和思考，有益于锻炼自己心气平和的能力，反正别人如何认为、如何评价、如何议论根本没办法影响一个人所处的状态。但是，一旦某个人开始为此心烦意乱、坐卧不安，甚至为此有一些无聊的举动，那么他就不仅是倒霉，而且是可怜了，因为他已经被别人左右了。

第8章 积累

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

愿上帝赐予我从容去接受我不能改变的，赐予我勇气去改变我可以改变的，并赐予我智慧去分辨这两者间的区别[插图]。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

相信积累的力量，本质上就是相信复利的力量。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

相信积累的人往往更容易获得财富和成就。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

富裕家庭能给孩子创造的环境，再对比一下贫困家庭能给孩子创造的环境，足以看出，从整体上来讲（注意，个别的反例并不能说明整体上的问题），贫与富的区别可能造成巨大的智力差异。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

如果能够彻底理解积累的重要，相信积累的力量，那么再进一步，就只有一个结论了：越早醒悟越好。

![underline](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAiIGhlaWdodD0iMjAiIHZpZXdCb3g9IjAgMCAyMCAyMCIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj4KPGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iMTAiIGN5PSIxMCIgcj0iMTAiIGZpbGw9IiM3Nzc3NzciIGZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eT0iMC4xNyIvPgo8cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTEzLjM1MDUgMTIuMDgzMkgxMi4xMDQ3TDExLjU3MzggMTAuNTM0SDguNTI5NjhMNy45OTg4NCAxMi4wODMySDYuNzUzMDFMOS41ODA1MSA0LjM2OTg3SDEwLjUyM0wxMy4zNTA1IDEyLjA4MzJaTTExLjI0ODggOS41MzczN0wxMC4wNzg4IDYuMTE0MDRMOC44NzYzNCA5LjUzNzM3SDExLjI0ODhaTTEzLjMzMzQgMTMuNzVINi42NjY3NVYxNUgxMy4zMzM0VjEzLjc1WiIgZmlsbD0iIzk5QTBBQSIvPgo8L3N2Zz4K)

想想看什么可以改变、什么不可以改变，找到能改变的领域，采取积累的策略，这是唯一的方法。每个人都必须为自己的过去埋单。

第1版推荐序

能够登上金字塔顶端的只有两种动物，一种是雄鹰，一种是蜗牛。
